class="mt-4 grid items-start gap-10 lg:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_auto]" data-testid="templates/details/content"><div class="order-2 lg:order-1"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal min-w-0 [&amp;&gt;*:first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*:last-child]:mb-0"><h2 class="mt-8 mb-4 text-[32px] leading-10 font-semibold tracking-[-0.79px]">Sales Call Summary Agent</h2>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">An AI-powered agent that automatically summarizes sales calls using Vercel&#x27;s Sandbox architecture. The agent analyzes call transcripts and generates structured summaries with objections, action items, and insights.</p>
<blockquote class="my-4 border-muted-foreground/30 border-l-4 pl-4 text-muted-foreground italic" data-streamdown="blockquote">
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Template Note</span>: This template uses <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Gong</span> as a starting example for call transcript integration. You can adapt it to work with other call recording platforms (Zoom, Google Meet, etc.) by modifying the webhook handler and transcript fetching logic.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote class="my-4 border-muted-foreground/30 border-l-4 pl-4 text-muted-foreground italic" data-streamdown="blockquote">
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Extensible</span>: This template can be extended to integrate with Salesforce (or another CRM of your choice), Slack (to post call summaries), and other services. The demo files in <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/demo-files/context/</code> demonstrate how CRM data and other context can be provided to the agent.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Features</h3>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Structured Summaries</span> - AI-generated summaries with tasks, objections, and key insights</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Sandbox Agent</span> - Uses Vercel Sandbox for secure code execution and file exploration</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">bash-tool</a></span> - Generic bash tool for AI agents, compatible with AI SDK</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Demo Mode</span> - Works out of the box with mock data (no Gong credentials needed)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Objection Tracking</span> - Identifies and scores how well objections were handled</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Durable Workflows</span> - Built with Vercel Workflow DevKit for reliability</li>
</ul>
<hr class="my-6 border-border" data-streamdown="horizontal-rule"/>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">One-Click Deploy (Demo Mode)</h3>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">You can deploy to Vercel and try it immediately with demo data with one click:</p>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><a href="https://vercel.com/new/clone?build-command=npm%20run%20build&amp;demo-description=Build%20an%20AI%20agent%20to%20analyze%20sales%20call%20data%20using%20Vercel%20Sandbox%20and%20AI%20SDK.%20Features%20secure%20code%20execution%20and%20durable%20workflows.&amp;demo-image=%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fe5382hct74si%2F2YZvDQ9gCIBnjtV7hSZq4s%2F2759b0c065ad8a0627b24468bc7753fe%2FImage.png&amp;demo-title=Call%20Summary%20AI%20Agent&amp;demo-url=https%3A%2F%2Fcall-summary-agent-demo.labs.vercel.dev%2F&amp;from=templates&amp;install-command=npm%20install&amp;project-name=Call%20Summary%20AI%20Agent&amp;project-names=Comma%20separated%20list%20of%20project%20names%2Cto%20match%20the%20root-directories&amp;repository-name=call-summary-agent&amp;repository-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-labs%2Fcall-summary-agent-with-sandbox&amp;root-directories=List%20of%20directory%20paths%20for%20the%20directories%20to%20clone%20into%20projects&amp;skippable-integrations=1&amp;teamSlug=andrewqu" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"></a></p>
<blockquote class="my-4 border-muted-foreground/30 border-l-4 pl-4 text-muted-foreground italic" data-streamdown="blockquote">
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Demo mode is <span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">enabled by default</span> - no Gong credentials required to test!</p>
</blockquote>
<hr class="my-6 border-border" data-streamdown="horizontal-rule"/>

<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Production Setup (Real Gong Data)</h3>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">To use real Gong API data instead of demo data:</p>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">1. Set Environment Variables</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Add these to your Vercel project settings or <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">.env.local</code>:</p>

<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Note:</span> Demo mode is automatically enabled when Gong credentials are missing.</p>
</blockquote>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">2. Configure Gong Webhook</h4>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Go to your Gong settings &gt; Integrations &gt; Webhooks</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Create a new webhook with:
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">URL</span>: <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">https://your-app.vercel.app/api/gong-webhook</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Events</span>: Select &quot;Call completed&quot;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Save and test the webhook</li>
</ol>
<hr class="my-6 border-border" data-streamdown="horizontal-rule"/>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Architecture</h3>
<pre><div class="my-4 w-full overflow-auto" data-testid="templates/details/mermaid"><div class="w-full [&amp;&gt;svg]:h-auto [&amp;&gt;svg]:w-full" style="display:none"></div><div class="text-copy-14 py-3 text-gray-700">Loading diagram...</div></div></pre>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Environment Variables</h3>





























<div class="@container pointer-events-none w-full overflow-visible"><div class="table-module__jeZm6q__tableContainer"><table class="table-module__jeZm6q__docsTable pointer-events-auto w-full overflow-visible"><thead><tr aria-roledescription="row" class="row"><th>Variable</th><th>Required</th><th>Default</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table-body-module__raQk9q__docsTbody"><tr aria-roledescription="row" class="row"><td><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">GONG_ACCESS_KEY</code></td><td>No</td><td>-</td><td>Gong API access key (demo mode if missing)</td></tr><tr aria-roledescription="row" class="row"><td><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">GONG_SECRET_KEY</code></td><td>No</td><td>-</td><td>Gong API secret key (demo mode if missing)</td></tr><tr aria-roledescription="row" class="row"><td><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">COMPANY_NAME</code></td><td>No</td><td>&quot;Your Company&quot;</td><td>Company name in prompts</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>

<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Configuration</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Custom System Prompt</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Override the default system prompt:</p>

<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">How It Works</h3>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Webhook Received</span>: Gong sends call data when a call completes (or mock data in demo mode)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Workflow Started</span>: The durable workflow begins processing</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Transcript Fetched</span>: Call transcript is retrieved from Gong API (or mock data)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Sandbox Created</span>: A secure sandbox is created with call files</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Agent Runs</span>: The AI agent explores transcripts using <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">bash-tool</a></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Summary Generated</span>: Structured output with tasks, objections, insights</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Workflow Steps</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Each step uses the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">&quot;use step&quot;</code> directive for:</p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Automatic retries on failure</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">State persistence</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Observability in Vercel dashboard</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Sandbox Tools</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">The agent uses <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">bash-tool</a> for exploring call transcripts via shell commands:</p>

<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Customization</h3>

<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">API Reference</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">POST /api/gong-webhook</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Receives Gong webhook payloads and triggers the summary workflow.</p>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Request Body</span>: Gong webhook payload or empty <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">{}</code> in demo mode.</p>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Response</span>:</p>
<pre><div class="relative rounded-md border border-[var(--ds-gray-400)] overflow-hidden group/copy my-4 h-auto language-json" data-geist-code-block=""><button type="button" tabindex="0" data-react-aria-pressable="true" aria-label="Copy to clipboard" data-testid="copy/button" class="outline-none m-0 border-0 align-baseline no-underline group/trigger relative cursor-pointer select-none aria-disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:text-[var(--ds-gray-700)] disabled:bg-[var(--ds-gray-100)] aria-disabled:text-[var(--ds-gray-700)] aria-disabled:bg-[var(--ds-gray-100)] disabled:![--themed-border:_var(--ds-gray-400)] [--x-padding:10px] [--height:40px] text-[14px] rounded-md [--themed-bg:_var(--ds-background-100)] shadow-[0_0_0_1px_var(--themed-border,_transparent)] <h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Output</h3>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">The function returns a string output which can be configured into an outputSchema of your choice.</p>

Sales Call Summary Agent\n\nAn AI-powered agent that automatically summarizes sales calls using Vercel's Sandbox architecture. The agent analyzes call transcripts and generates structured summaries with objections, action items, and insights.\n\n\u003e **Template Note**: This template uses **Gong** as a starting example for call transcript integration. You can adapt it to work with other call recording platforms (Zoom, Google Meet, etc.) by modifying the webhook handler and transcript fetching logic.\n\n\u003e **Extensible**: This template can be extended to integrate with Salesforce (or another CRM of your choice), Slack (to post call summaries), and other services. The demo files in `/demo-files/context/` demonstrate how CRM data and other context can be provided to the agent.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Structured Summaries** - AI-generated summaries with tasks, objections, and key insights\n- **Sandbox Agent** - Uses Vercel Sandbox for secure code execution and file exploration\n- **[bash-tool](https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool)** - Generic bash tool for AI agents, compatible with AI SDK\n- **Demo Mode** - Works out of the box with mock data (no Gong credentials needed)\n- **Objection Tracking** - Identifies and scores how well objections were handled\n- **Durable Workflows** - Built with Vercel Workflow DevKit for reliability\n\n---\n\n## One-Click Deploy (Demo Mode)\n\nYou can deploy to Vercel and try it immediately with demo data with one click:\n\n[![Deploy with Vercel](https://vercel.com/button)](https://vercel.com/new/clone?build-command=npm%20run%20build\u0026demo-description=Build%20an%20AI%20agent%20to%20analyze%20sales%20call%20data%20using%20Vercel%20Sandbox%20and%20AI%20SDK.%20Features%20secure%20code%20execution%20and%20durable%20workflows.\u0026demo-image=%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fe5382hct74si%2F2YZvDQ9gCIBnjtV7hSZq4s%2F2759b0c065ad8a0627b24468bc7753fe%2FImage.png\u0026demo-title=Call%20Summary%20AI%20Agent\u0026demo-url=https%3A%2F%2Fcall-summary-agent-demo.labs.vercel.dev%2F\u0026from=templates\u0026install-command=npm%20install\u0026project-name=Call%20Summary%20AI%20Agent\u0026project-names=Comma%20separated%20list%20of%20project%20names%2Cto%20match%20the%20root-directories\u0026repository-name=call-summary-agent\u0026repository-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-labs%2Fcall-summary-agent-with-sandbox\u0026root-directories=List%20of%20directory%20paths%20for%20the%20directories%20to%20clone%20into%20projects\u0026skippable-integrations=1\u0026teamSlug=andrewqu)\n\n\n\u003e Demo mode is **enabled by default** - no Gong credentials required to test!\n\n---\n\n## Local Development (Demo Mode)\n\n### 1. Clone and Install\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/vercel-labs/call-summary-agent\ncd call-summary-agent\npnpm install\n```\n\n### 2. Link to Vercel (creates .env.local automatically)\n\n```bash\nvercel link\nvercel env pull\n```\n\n### 3. Run\n\n```bash\npnpm dev\n```\n\n### 4. Test\n\n```bash\n# Trigger the agent with demo data\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:3000/api/gong-webhook \\\n  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n  -d '{}'\n```\n\n---\n\n## Production Setup (Real Gong Data)\n\nTo use real Gong API data instead of demo data:\n\n### 1. Set Environment Variables\n\nAdd these to your Vercel project settings or `.env.local`:\n\n| Variable | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `GONG_ACCESS_KEY` | Yes | Your Gong API access key |\n| `GONG_SECRET_KEY` | Yes | Your Gong API secret key |\n\n```bash\nGONG_ACCESS_KEY=your_gong_access_key\nGONG_SECRET_KEY=your_gong_secret_key\n```\n\n\u003e **Note:** Demo mode is automatically enabled when Gong credentials are missing.\n\n### 2. Configure Gong Webhook\n\n1. Go to your Gong settings \u003e Integrations \u003e Webhooks\n2. Create a new webhook with:\n   - **URL**: `https://your-app.vercel.app/api/gong-webhook`\n   - **Events**: Select \"Call completed\"\n3. Save and test the webhook\n\n---\n\n## Architecture\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    subgraph entry [Entry Point]\n        Webhook[POST /api/gong-webhook]\n    end\n\n    subgraph workflow [Workflow Layer]\n        WF[\"workflowGongSummary\u003cbr/\u003e(use workflow)\"]\n        Steps[\"Workflow Steps\u003cbr/\u003e(use step)\"]\n    end\n\n    subgraph agent [Agent Layer]\n        Agent[ToolLoopAgent]\n        Sandbox[Vercel Sandbox]\n    end\n\n    subgraph tools [Sandbox Tools]\n        Bash[bash-tool]\n    end\n\n    subgraph external [External Services]\n        Gong[Gong API]\n    end\n\n    Webhook --\u003e WF\n    WF --\u003e Steps\n    Steps --\u003e Agent\n    Agent --\u003e Sandbox\n    Agent --\u003e tools\n    Steps --\u003e Gong\n```\n\n## Environment Variables\n\n| Variable | Required | Default | Description |\n|----------|----------|---------|-------------|\n| `GONG_ACCESS_KEY` | No | - | Gong API access key (demo mode if missing) |\n| `GONG_SECRET_KEY` | No | - | Gong API secret key (demo mode if missing) |\n| `COMPANY_NAME` | No | \"Your Company\" | Company name in prompts |\n\n## Demo Mode Details\n\nDemo mode uses realistic mock data including a sample 20-minute product demo call. The demo files are organized in the `/demo-files` folder:\n\n```\ndemo-files/\n├── webhook-data.json              # Mock Gong webhook payload\n├── transcript.json                # 20-minute call transcript\n└── context/\n    ├── gong-calls/previous/       # Historical calls\n    │   ├── demo-call-000-discovery-call.md\n    │   └── demo-call-intro-initial-call.md\n    ├── research/                  # Background info\n    │   ├── company-research.md\n    │   └── competitive-intel.md\n    └── playbooks/\n        └── sales-playbook.md\n```\n\nThese files are loaded into the sandbox for the agent to explore.\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Custom System Prompt\n\nOverride the default system prompt:\n\n```bash\nAGENT_SYSTEM_PROMPT=\"You are a sales call analyst...\"\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. **Webhook Received**: Gong sends call data when a call completes (or mock data in demo mode)\n2. **Workflow Started**: The durable workflow begins processing\n3. **Transcript Fetched**: Call transcript is retrieved from Gong API (or mock data)\n4. **Sandbox Created**: A secure sandbox is created with call files\n5. **Agent Runs**: The AI agent explores transcripts using [bash-tool](https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool)\n6. **Summary Generated**: Structured output with tasks, objections, insights\n\n### Workflow Steps\n\nEach step uses the `\"use step\"` directive for:\n- Automatic retries on failure\n- State persistence\n- Observability in Vercel dashboard\n\n### Sandbox Tools\n\nThe agent uses [bash-tool](https://www.npmjs.com/package/bash-tool) for exploring call transcripts via shell commands:\n\n```bash\n# List call files\nls gong-calls/\n\n# Search for pricing discussions\ngrep -r \"pricing\" gong-calls/\n\n# View call metadata\ncat gong-calls/metadata.json\n\n# Find objections\ngrep -i \"concern\\|issue\\|problem\" gong-calls/*.md\n```\n\nAll bash commands are logged for observability:\n```\n[bash-tool] INFO: Bash command starting { command: 'grep -r \"pricing\" gong-calls/' }\n[bash-tool] INFO: Bash command completed { command: '...', exitCode: 0, stdoutLength: 605 }\n```\n\n## Output Schema\n\nThe agent generates structured output:\n\n```typescript\n{\n  summary: string,           // Comprehensive call summary\n  tasks: [{\n    taskDescription: string,\n    taskOwner: string,\n    ownerCompany: 'internal' | 'customer' | 'partner'\n  }],\n  objections: [{\n    description: string,\n    quote: string,\n    speaker: string,\n    speakerCompany: string,\n    handled: boolean,\n    handledAnswer: string,\n    handledScore: number,    // 0-100\n    handledBy: string\n  }]\n}\n```\n\n## Customization\n\n### Custom Playbooks\n\nAdd playbook detection by configuring `config.playbooks` in `lib/config.ts`.\n\n## Development\n\n```bash\n# Install dependencies\npnpm install\n\n# Run development server\npnpm dev\n\n# Build for production\npnpm build\n```\n\n## Project Structure\n\n```\nsales-call-summary-agent/\n├── app/\n│   ├── api/gong-webhook/    # Webhook endpoint\n│   ├── layout.tsx\n│   └── page.tsx             # Status page\n├── demo-files/              # Demo mode files\n│   ├── webhook-data.json\n│   ├── transcript.json\n│   └── context/             # Additional context files\n├── lib/\n│   ├── agent.ts             # ToolLoopAgent configuration\n│   ├── config.ts            # Centralized configuration\n│   ├── gong-client.ts       # Gong API helpers\n│   ├── mock-data.ts         # Demo mode loader\n│   ├── sandbox-context.ts   # File generation for sandbox\n│   ├── tools.ts             # Agent tools (bash-tool)\n│   ├── types.ts             # TypeScript types\n│   └── logger.ts            # Logging utility\n└── workflows/\n    └── gong-summary/\n        ├── index.ts         # Main workflow\n        └── steps.ts         # Workflow steps\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### POST /api/gong-webhook\n\nReceives Gong webhook payloads and triggers the summary workflow.\n\n**Request Body**: Gong webhook payload or empty `{}` in demo mode.\n\n**Response**:\n```json\n{\n  \"message\": \"Workflow triggered\",\n  \"callId\": \"1234567890\"\n}\n```\n\n## Output\nThe function returns a string output which can be configured into an outputSchema of your choice.\n\n## Contributing\n\nContributions are welcome! Please open an issue or submit a pull request.\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"40:[\"$\",\"$L4c\",null,{\"githubUrl\":\"https://github.com/vercel-labs/call-summary-agent-with-sandbox\",\"readmeText\":\"$4d\"}]\n42:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"flex w-full flex-row items-center gap-4 lg:flex-col lg:items-start\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"className\":\"text-gray-1000 text-md shrink-0 font-medium\",\"children\":\"License\"}],[\"$\",\"$L27\",null,{\"className\":\"text-sm font-medium text-nowrap text-(--geist-link-color)! no-underline underline-offset-4 hover:underline\",\"href\":\"https://github.com/vercel-labs/call-summary-agent-with-sandbox/blob/main/LICENSE\",\"children\":\"View License\"}]]}]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"21:null\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"26:[[\"$\",\"title\",\"0\",{\"children\":\"Sales Call AI Summary Agent with Vercel Sandbox, AI SDK.
